   127	                    numOfInvalidFiles === 1 ? 'singular' : 'plural'

   132	                  messages,
   133	                  values: {

   136	                  },

   161	      const themeProp = theme.fileInput[propertyName];
   162	      if (themeProp)

   164	          if (defaultKey) result[defaultKey] = themeProp;
   165	          else result = themeProp;
   166	        else result = { ...themeProp };

   245	      const dt = new DataTransfer();
   246	      const curFiles = inputRef.current.files;
   247	      if (index === 'all' || nextFiles.length === 0)
   248	        inputRef.current.value = '';
   249	      for (let i = 0; i < curFiles.length; i += 1) {
   250	        const curfile = curFiles[i];
   251	        if (index !== i) dt.items.add(curfile);
   252	      }

   254	      const nativeInputValueSetter = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(
   255	        window.HTMLInputElement.prototype,
   256	        'files',
   257	      ).set;
   258	      nativeInputValueSetter.call(inputRef.current, dt.files);
   259	      const event = new Event('input', { bubbles: true });
   260	      inputRef.current.dispatchEvent(event);
   261

   264	    };

    40	const RelativeBox = styled(Box)`
    41	  position: relative;
    42	`;

    44	// We have two Styled* components to separate
    45	// the newer default|primary|secondary approach,
    46	// which we use the term "kind" to refer to,
    47	// from the previous approach. Hopefully, when we get to grommet v3,
    48	// we can drop the old way and just use kind.
    49	//
    50	// In the kind approach, we rely on the basic structure of the theme
    51	// being repeated. For example: button.default, button.active,
    52	// button.active.default all refer to a similar object containing
    53	// { background, border, color, padding }.
    54	// This allows us to use the same code to evaluate color and generate CSS.
    55	// We just need to build up CSS, since selectors override previous ones.
    56	// See StyledButtonKind.kindStyles() for this.
    57	// And we build down to determine icon color, once we have a color from
    58	// the latest applicable state, we can stop. See Button.getIconColor() for this.
    59	// backgroundAndTextColor() is used in both cases to ensure we are determining
    60	// color in the same way, so the icon and label align.
    61	
    62	// only when default is in the theme
    63	// Used to get the color for the icon to match what StyledButtonKind
    64	// and backgroundStyle() will do for the label.
    65	// The paths are ordered from basic to specific. Go through them
    66	// specific to base until we find one that has a color and use that.
    67	const getIconColor = (paths = [], theme, colorProp, kind) => {
    68	  let result = [];
    69	  let index = paths.length - 1;
    70	  // caller has specified a themeObj to use for styling
    71	  // relevant for cases like pagination which looks to theme.pagination.button
    72	  if (typeof kind === 'object') index = 0;
    73	  // stop when we have a color or no more paths
    74	  while (index >= 0 && !result[1]) {
    75	    const baseObj = (typeof kind === 'object' && kind) || theme.button;
    76	    let obj = baseObj;
    77	    // find sub-object under the button theme that corresponds with this path
    78	    // for example: 'active.primary'
    79	    if (paths[index]) {
    80	      const parts = paths[index].split('.');
    81	      while (obj && parts.length) obj = obj[parts.shift()];
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    if (obj) {
    85	      // use passed in color for background if the theme has a background color
    86	      const background =
    87	        colorProp && obj.background && obj.background.color
    88	          ? colorProp
    89	          : obj.background;
    90	
    91	      // if theme object explicitly sets the color to undefined, pass false
    92	      // to indicate that the theme doesn't want any text color
    93	      const objColor =
    94	        obj.color ||
    95	        (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, 'color') &&
    96	        obj.color === undefined
    97	          ? false
    98	          : undefined);
    99	
   100	      let color;
   101	      if (obj?.icon?.props?.color) color = obj.icon.props.color;
   102	      // if no icon defined for this state, see if there is an icon
   103	      // with color defined at one higher level
   104	      else if (paths[index + 1]) {
   105	        const parts = paths[index + 1].split('.');
   106	        while (baseObj && parts.length) obj = baseObj[parts.shift()];
   107	        if (obj?.icon?.props?.color) color = obj.icon.props.color;
   108	      }
   109	      // use passed in color for text if the theme doesn't have
   110	      // background or border color
   111	      if (!color)
   112	        color =
   113	          colorProp &&
   114	          (!obj.background || !obj.background.color) &&
   115	          (!obj.border || !obj.border.color)
   116	            ? colorProp
   117	            : objColor;
   118	
   119	      result = backgroundAndTextColors(background, color, theme);
   120	    }
   121	    index -= 1;
   122	  }
   123	  return result[1] || undefined;
   124	};
   125	
   126	// get the icon for the current button state
   127	const getKindIcon = (paths = [], theme, kind) => {
   128	  let result;
   129	  let index = paths.length - 1;
   130	  // caller has specified a themeObj to use for styling
   131	  // relevant for cases like pagination which looks to theme.pagination.button
   132	  if (typeof kind === 'object') index = 0;
   133	  // stop when we have a color or no more paths
   134	  while (index >= 0 && !result) {
   135	    let obj = (typeof kind === 'object' && kind) || theme.button;
   136	    // find sub-object under the button theme that corresponds with this path
   137	    // for example: 'active.primary'
   138	    if (paths[index]) {
   139	      const parts = paths[index].split('.');
   140	      while (obj && parts.length) obj = obj[parts.shift()];
   141	    }

   146	  }

   150	const getPropertyColor = (property, paths = [], theme, kind, primary) => {
   151	  let result;
   152	  if (kind) {
   153	    let obj = (typeof kind === 'object' && kind) || theme.button;

for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
  const line = lines[i];
  if (line.includes('"'"'fileInput.browse'"'"')) {
    let occurrence = {
      lineNumber: i + 1,
      type: line.includes('"'"'<Button'"'"') ? '"'"'Button'"'"' : '"'"'Anchor'"'"',
      hasDisabled: false,
      content: line
    };

    let componentContent = line;
    let j = i;

      if (j - i > 20) break;
    }

@@ -0,0 +1,98 @@
+// Detailed verification of the disabled prop fix
+const fs = require('fs');
+
+const content = fs.readFileSync('/testbed/src/js/components/FileInput/FileInput.js', 'utf8');
+
+console.log('=== DETAILED VERIFICATION OF FILEINPUT DISABLED PROP ===\n');
+
+// Find all browse button/anchor occurrences with their disabled status
+const browseOccurrences = [];
+const lines = content.split('\n');
+
+for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
+  const line = lines[i];
+  if (line.includes('fileInput.browse')) {
+    let occurrence = {
+      lineNumber: i + 1,
+      type: line.includes('<Button') ? 'Button' : 'Anchor',
+      hasDisabled: false,
+      content: line
+    };
+    
+    // Check current component for disabled prop
+    let componentContent = line;
+    let j = i;
+    
+    // Traverse until we find the closing tag or end of component
+    while (j < lines.length && !componentContent.includes('/>') && !componentContent.includes('</')) {
+      j++;
+      componentContent += ' ' + lines[j];
+      
+      // Safety check to avoid infinite loop
+      if (j - i > 20) break;
+    }
+    
+    occurrence.hasDisabled = componentContent.includes('disabled={disabled}');
+    occurrence.fullContent = componentContent;
+    browseOccurrences.push(occurrence);
+  }
+}
+
+console.log(`Found ${browseOccurrences.length} browse controls:\n`);
+
+let buttonCount = 0;
+let anchorCount = 0;
+let buttonsWithDisabled = 0;
+let anchorsWithDisabled = 0;
+
+browseOccurrences.forEach((occ, index) => {
+  console.log(`📍 Occurrence ${index + 1}:`);
+  console.log(`   Type: ${occ.type}`);
+  console.log(`   Line: ${occ.lineNumber}`);
+  console.log(`   Has disabled prop: ${occ.hasDisabled ? '✅ YES' : '❌ NO'}`);
+  console.log(`   Content snippet: ${occ.content.substring(0, 100)}...\n`);
+  
+  if (occ.type === 'Button') {
+    buttonCount++;
+    if (occ.hasDisabled) buttonsWithDisabled++;
+  } else {
+    anchorCount++;
+    if (occ.hasDisabled) anchorsWithDisabled++;
+  }
+});
+
+console.log('\n=== SUMMARY ===\n');
+console.log(`Browse Buttons: ${buttonsWithDisabled}/${buttonCount} have disabled prop`);
+console.log(`Browse Anchors: ${anchorsWithDisabled}/${anchorCount} have disabled prop\n`);
+
+// Verify all three UI states have proper disabled props
+const expectedCount = 3; // 3 UI states
+
+if (buttonsWithDisabled >= expectedCount && anchorsWithDisabled >= expectedCount) {
+  console.log('🎉 SUCCESS! All browse controls have disabled prop.');
+  console.log('The PR requirement has been fully satisfied.');
+} else {
+  console.log('❌ INCOMPLETE! Some browse controls are missing disabled prop.');
+  console.log(`Expected minimum: ${expectedCount} of each type`);
+}
+
+// Also verify that disabled styling is properly applied
+console.log('\n=== ADDITIONAL CHECKS ===\n');
+
+// Check if ContentsBox has disabled styling
+const contentsBoxHasDisabled = content.includes('ContentsBox') && 
+                               content.includes('disabled={disabled}') &&
+                               content.includes('disabled && disabledStyle()');
+console.log(`ContentsBox disabled styling: ${contentsBoxHasDisabled ? '✅ Present' : '❌ Missing'}`);
+
+// Check if input element has disabled prop
+const inputHasDisabled = content.includes('<StyledFileInput') && 
+                         content.includes('disabled={disabled}');
+console.log(`Input element disabled prop: ${inputHasDisabled ? '✅ Present' : '❌ Missing'}`);
+
+// Check if remove buttons have disabled props
+const removeButtonPattern = /<Button[\s\S]*?removeAll[\s\S]*?disabled=\{disabled\}/g;
+const removeButtonsWithDisabled = (content.match(removeButtonPattern) || []).length;
+console.log(`Remove buttons with disabled prop: ${removeButtonsWithDisabled} found`);
+
+console.log('\n=== VERIFICATION COMPLETE ===');

+// Test edge cases for FileInput disabled prop
+const fs = require('fs');
+
+const fileContent = fs.readFileSync('/testbed/src/js/components/FileInput/FileInput.js', 'utf8');
+
+console.log('=== TESTING EDGE CASES ===\n');
+
+// Test 1: Verify onClick handlers properly handle disabled state
+console.log('Test 1: Checking if onClick handlers are properly conditional when disabled');
+
+const onClickHandlerPattern = /onClick=\{\(\)\s*=>\s*{\s*inputRef\.current\.click\(\);\s*inputRef\.current\.focus\(\);\s*}\s*}/g;
+const onClickHandlers = fileContent.match(onClickHandlerPattern) || [];
+console.log(`✅ Found ${onClickHandlers.length} onClick handlers for browse button/anchor`);
+
+// Check that the onClick handlers are NOT wrapped in disabled condition
+// This is correct because the disabled prop itself will prevent the onClick from firing
+const onClickWrappedInDisabled = fileContent.match(/disabled\s*\?\s*undefined\s*:\s*\(\)\s*=>\s*{\s*inputRef\.current\.click\(\)/g) || [];
+if (onClickWrappedInDisabled.length === 0) {
+  console.log('✅ onClick handlers are NOT wrapped in disabled condition (correct - handled by disabled prop itself)');
+} else {
+  console.log('❌ onClick handlers are wrapped in disabled condition (should be handled by disabled prop)');
+}
+
+// Test 2: Verify that MouseOver/MouseOut handlers properly handle disabled state
+console.log('\nTest 2: Checking MouseOver/MouseOut handlers for disabled state');
+const mouseOverDisabledCount = (fileContent.match(/onMouseOver=\{disabled \? undefined/gi) || []).length;
+const mouseOutDisabledCount = (fileContent.match(/onMouseOut=\{disabled \? undefined/gi) || []).length;
+
+if (mouseOverDisabledCount >= 1 && mouseOutDisabledCount >= 1) {
+  console.log('✅ MouseOver/MouseOut handlers properly handle disabled state');
+} else {
+  console.log('❌ MouseOver/MouseOut handlers may not properly handle disabled state');
+}
+
+// Test 3: Verify that all browse Button/Anchor instances have consistent structure
+console.log('\nTest 3: Checking consistency across all browse Button/Anchor instances');
+
+// Check that all browse buttons follow the same pattern
+const browseButtonPattern = /<Button[^>]*tabIndex=\{-1\}[^>]*ref=\{controlRef\}[^>]*kind=\{theme\.fileInput\.button\}[^>]*label=[^>]*fileInput\.browse[^>]*onClick=[^>]*disabled=\{disabled\}[^>]*\/>/g;
+const browseAnchorPattern = /<Anchor[^>]*tabIndex=\{-1\}[^>]*(alignSelf="center")?[^>]*ref=\{controlRef\}[^>]*margin="small"[^>]*onClick=[^>]*label=[^>]*fileInput\.browse[^>]*disabled=\{disabled\}[^>]*\/>/g;
+
+const consistentButtons = (fileContent.match(browseButtonPattern) || []).length;
+const consistentAnchors = (fileContent.match(browseAnchorPattern) || []).length;
+
+console.log(`✅ Found ${consistentButtons} browse Button instances with consistent structure`);
+console.log(`✅ Found ${consistentAnchors} browse Anchor instances with consistent structure`);
+
+// Test 4: Verify that the core input element also receives disabled prop
+console.log('\nTest 4: Checking if the main input element receives disabled prop');
+const inputDisabled = fileContent.includes('<StyledFileInput') && fileContent.includes('disabled={disabled}');
+if (inputDisabled) {
+  console.log('✅ Main file input element receives disabled prop');
+} else {
+  console.log('❌ Main file input element may not receive disabled prop');
+}
+
+// Test 5: Verify that remove buttons also receive disabled prop
+console.log('\nTest 5: Checking if remove buttons also receive disabled prop');
+const removeButtonPattern = /<Button[^>]*removeAll[^>]*disabled=\{disabled\}/g;
+const removeButtonsWithDisabled = (fileContent.match(removeButtonPattern) || []).length;
+
+if (removeButtonsWithDisabled >= 2) { // At least 2 remove buttons should have disabled prop
+  console.log('✅ Remove buttons also receive disabled prop (correct for consistency)');
+} else {
+  console.log('⚠️ Remove buttons may not all receive disabled prop');
+}
+
+console.log('\n=== EDGE CASE TESTING COMPLETE ===\n');
+
+// Overall assessment
+const totalBrowseControlsWithDisabled = consistentButtons + consistentAnchors;
+if (totalBrowseControlsWithDisabled >= 6) { // 3 buttons + 3 anchors
+  console.log('🎉 OVERALL SUCCESS: All edge cases handled correctly!');

+// Verify that the disabled prop is properly passed to browse Button/Anchor
+const fs = require('fs');
+
+const fileContent = fs.readFileSync('/testbed/src/js/components/FileInput/FileInput.js', 'utf8');
+
+console.log('=== VERIFICATION OF FIX ===');
+
+// Count all Button components with disabled prop
+const buttonDisabledMatches = fileContent.match(/<Button[\s\S]*?disabled={disabled}/g) || [];
+console.log(`✅ Found ${buttonDisabledMatches.length} Button components with disabled prop`);
+
+// Count all Anchor components with disabled prop  
+const anchorDisabledMatches = fileContent.match(/<Anchor[\s\S]*?disabled={disabled}/g) || [];
+console.log(`✅ Found ${anchorDisabledMatches.length} Anchor components with disabled prop`);
+
+// Specifically check for browse Button components with disabled prop
+const browseButtonMatches = fileContent.match(/<Button[\s\S]*?fileInput\.browse[\s\S]*?disabled={disabled}/g) || [];
+console.log(`✅ Found ${browseButtonMatches.length} browse Button components with disabled prop`);
+
+// Specifically check for browse Anchor components with disabled prop
+const browseAnchorMatches = fileContent.match(/<Anchor[\s\S]*?fileInput\.browse[\s\S]*?disabled={disabled}/g) || [];
+console.log(`✅ Found ${browseAnchorMatches.length} browse Anchor components with disabled prop`);
+
+// Expected: 3 of each (since there are 3 different UI states where browse button/anchor appear)
+const totalExpected = 3;
+
+if (browseButtonMatches.length >= totalExpected && browseAnchorMatches.length >= totalExpected) {
+  console.log('\n🎉 SUCCESS: All browse Button/Anchor components now receive the disabled prop!');
+  console.log('The fix has been properly implemented according to the PR requirements.');
+  
+  // Confirm the specific locations where it was added
+  const browseButtonLocations = fileContent.split('\n').reduce((acc, line, index) => {
+    if (line.includes('fileInput.browse') && line.includes('Button') && line.includes('disabled')) {
+      acc.push(`Line ${index + 1}`);
+    }
+    return acc;
+  }, []);
+  
+  const browseAnchorLocations = fileContent.split('\n').reduce((acc, line, index) => {
+    if (line.includes('fileInput.browse') && line.includes('Anchor') && line.includes('disabled')) {
+      acc.push(`Line ${index + 1}`);
+    }
+    return acc;
+  }, []);
+  
+  console.log(`\nBrowse Button with disabled prop found at:`);
+  browseButtonLocations.forEach(loc => console.log(`  - ${loc}`));
+  
+  console.log(`\nBrowse Anchor with disabled prop found at:`);
+  browseAnchorLocations.forEach(loc => console.log(`  - ${loc}`));
+  
+} else {
+  console.log('❌ FAILURE: Browse Button/Anchor components do not all receive disabled prop');
+  console.log(`Expected at least ${totalExpected} of each, but got:`);
+  console.log(`  - Browse Buttons: ${browseButtonMatches.length}`);
+  console.log(`  - Browse Anchors: ${browseAnchorMatches.length}`);
+}
+
+console.log('\n=== FIX VERIFICATION COMPLETE ===');
